- O
based B
collaborative O
filtering O
approach O
. O

Our O
system O
uses O
champion B
mastery O
points B
to O
indicate O
player B
preferences O
. O

We O
conducted O
a O
preliminary O
user B
study O
that O
validates O
the O
practicality O
of O
our O
system O
and O
indicates O
that O
users B
enjoy O
our O
system O
’s O
recommendations O
significantly O
more O
than O
random O
recommendations O
. O

In O
the O
future O
, O
we O
plan O
to O
rerun O
our O
survey O
study O
using O
optimal O
parameters O
. O

The O
recommender O
tested O
in O
our O
user B
study O
made O
use O
of O
the O
naive O
SVD O
model O
in O

Surprise O
library O
. O

The O
default O
parameters O
are O
[ O
15 O
] O
: O
epoch O
= O
20 O
, O
λ O
= O
0.005 O
, O

γ O
= O
0.02 O
, O

learning O
rate O
. O

The O
results O

in O
our O
preliminary O
study O
indicated O
that O
the O
SVD O
model O
is O
appropriate O
for O
a O

recommender O
system O
. O

Following O
this O
validation O
, O
we O
tuned O
these O
model O
parameters O
using O
a O
grid O
search O
to O
maximize O
theoretical O
accuracy O
by O
minimizing O
root O
mean O
square O
error O
[ O
15 O
] O
. O

The O
optimal O
parameters O
found O
are O
the O
following O
: O
epoch O
= O
20 O
, O
λ O
= O
0.4 O
, O
and O
γ O
= O
0.0005 O
. O

By O

these O
parameters O
for O
model O
fitting O
, O

results O

a O

would O

. O

Furthermore O
, O
to O

to O
individual B

player I

could O

of O
reference O
